    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

        <a title="Ella James" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ella James" href="/user/show/13035437-ella-james">Ella James</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2940438092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8310331823174311749">Caged Lions Never Roar by Arthur Archambeau is a beautiful, meaningful and old fashioned love story with the promise of freedom. The liberty to live, love and be who you were born to be is the theme of this amazing 5 star book.<br/><br/>David and Hannah are an unlikely couple with real chemistry who deeply desire to be with one-another. David is a disenchanted and fed-up minister, while Hannah hates being a stripper at a gentlemen’s club, but she must pay the bills. They have a common love of animals and </span>
  <span id="freeText8310331823174311749" style="display:none">Caged Lions Never Roar by Arthur Archambeau is a beautiful, meaningful and old fashioned love story with the promise of freedom. The liberty to live, love and be who you were born to be is the theme of this amazing 5 star book.<br /><br />David and Hannah are an unlikely couple with real chemistry who deeply desire to be with one-another. David is a disenchanted and fed-up minister, while Hannah hates being a stripper at a gentlemen’s club, but she must pay the bills. They have a common love of animals and baseball. They first meet at a shabby roadside zoo where they discover the neglect and poor living conditions for two caged lions, Babs and Bobby. Moved with passion and concern for the animals, together David and Hannah decide to try to save Babs and Bobby, the caged lions who never roar.<br /><br />Caged Lions Never Roar is a wonderful story about two young people who fall in love at first sight. Their mutual desire to help the caged lions brought them together. But David feels trapped in his own life of being a priest who must deal with the hypocrisy and the politics of the church. Hannah also wants to be free to live the life she desires away from the life of a stripper – who must deal with the harassment of the men at the club. As the story progresses the situation and drama becomes tense, as David and Hannah’s relationship becomes the center of gossip on social media. Eventually, David must make a choice between living the priestly life, or being with the woman he loves – despite her profession and background. Readers will fall in love with these two delightful characters as they desperately fight for freedom for themselves and for the neglected caged lions. This story is sweet, compelling and very thought-provoking.<br /><br />Arthur Archambeau has done a remarkable job of writing a clever, meaningful tale with a powerful clear message that will pull at the reader’s heart strings. His characters are relatable, likable and well developed, causing readers to root for them throughout the entire story. The descriptive writing brings this story to life with the expressive narration and impressive dialog between the characters.<br /><br />Caged Lions Never Roar is a well written, fast-paced and captivating romance story with a stirring narrative and satisfying conclusion. Skillfully woven together with imagination and passion, it is one book which contemporary romance readers will love and revel in. A must read page-turner with irresistible characters and a distinctive refreshing storyline, Caged Lions Never Roar by Arthur Archambeau is sure to become a bestseller!</span>
  <a data-text-id="8310331823174311749" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3189678510?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mrs. Varela " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mrs. Varela " href="/user/show/2430315-mrs-varela">Mrs. Varela </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3189678510" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9128951424743067804">Caged Lions Never Roar by Arthur Archambeau is an intriguing modern love story. It begins when Hannah Cohen and David O’Malley meet at Captain Rupert’s Wildlife Wonderland Zoo and find that they share a love for animals. There are two lions, Bobby and Babs who are being mistreated by the zoo’s owner and Hannah wishes there were a way to save them. David suggests that the two begin a campaign to save them. At their first meeting to plan to their crusade to save the lions Hannah learns that David </span>
  <span id="freeText9128951424743067804" style="display:none">Caged Lions Never Roar by Arthur Archambeau is an intriguing modern love story. It begins when Hannah Cohen and David O’Malley meet at Captain Rupert’s Wildlife Wonderland Zoo and find that they share a love for animals. There are two lions, Bobby and Babs who are being mistreated by the zoo’s owner and Hannah wishes there were a way to save them. David suggests that the two begin a campaign to save them. At their first meeting to plan to their crusade to save the lions Hannah learns that David is an Anglican priest. Nonetheless, sparks immediately begin to fly between the two of them. As they share personal details about themselves, Hannah leaves out one detail, she is a stripper. David on the other hand reveals that he had been a minor league baseball player and discovers Hannah’s love for baseball which draws them even closer together. <br /><br />While their romance quickly evolves, it also becomes a public affair. David is constantly reprimanded by the Bishop overseeing the parish and expresses that his behavior does not represent the Church. Seeing these rebukes as petty and at times intrusive causes him conflicting feelings about his role in the Church. At the same time Hannah is considering quitting the job she hates as a stripper to do something she loves. Things change when David learns exactly what it is that Hannah does for a living and he has a problem reconciling the woman he loves with what she does at work. Soon after he is given an ultimatum, leave Hannah or leave his position at the church. Will this kind of love last?<br /><br />The author filled this story with realistic characters and events. The story is so engaging that readers will find it hard not to read it in one sitting. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9128951424743067804" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15722612963513793032"><strong>A feel good romance!</strong><br/><br/>This book: Caged Lions Never Roar by Arthur Archambeau, is a sweet love story that had me captivated from the moment I opened the cover. The story is about Hannah, who is a stripper at a gentlemen’s club and David who is a priest. Hannah really doesn’t like herself for what she does for a living currently hates how the men at the club treat her. She has an English degree and longs to be a writer but she has never believed in herself enough to follow her dreams. <br/>David is a for</span>
  <span id="freeText15722612963513793032" style="display:none"><strong>A feel good romance!</strong><br /><br />This book: Caged Lions Never Roar by Arthur Archambeau, is a sweet love story that had me captivated from the moment I opened the cover. The story is about Hannah, who is a stripper at a gentlemen’s club and David who is a priest. Hannah really doesn’t like herself for what she does for a living currently hates how the men at the club treat her. She has an English degree and longs to be a writer but she has never believed in herself enough to follow her dreams. <br />David is a former minor league baseball player, and is an ordained minister. David wishes things were different with his work as he is unable to help the community the way he wants due to politics within the church. This is a wonderful story of these two very different people with radically different backgrounds and beliefs who meet at a shabby sort of zoo and make a commitment together to help a pair of lions. The poor lions are being treated poorly and have deplorable living conditions and the shared passion over the lions turns into romance and passion between David and Hannah. Such similarities between Hannah and David and these lions being caged and not living to their full potential. David and Hannah are both figuratively caged as well being that they are not happy in their jobs and wish to be doing other things. This is a wonderful, feel good romance and I highly recommend this read. You will enjoy it, and it will lift your spirits as well as reignite your hope and belief in the power of love. </span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3111802891?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Callie Wise" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Callie Wise" href="/user/show/23057637-callie-wise">Callie Wise</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3111802891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6231015051565599246">If you long for a sexy but romantic tale of love, hope, and second chances, then Caged Lions Never Roar is the perfect read for you. Typically, I’m not much for overly romantic love stories, but the writer struck a great balance. Hannah and David were two characters I could root for because they were trapped by lives neither wanted. I was eager to see how the writer would resolve the problems Hannah and David faced in their relationship, their own personal lives, and the background story of the </span>
  <span id="freeText6231015051565599246" style="display:none">If you long for a sexy but romantic tale of love, hope, and second chances, then Caged Lions Never Roar is the perfect read for you. Typically, I’m not much for overly romantic love stories, but the writer struck a great balance. Hannah and David were two characters I could root for because they were trapped by lives neither wanted. I was eager to see how the writer would resolve the problems Hannah and David faced in their relationship, their own personal lives, and the background story of the two lions that brought them together.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6231015051565599246" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('x0J2WU324BLvJzl17teMrV3+5jl3AcMxr2w0pT7dFa+XzFRDdF73zW/UASyT3+T/xvA93tWUSZBQ75tmdEj1Fw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZMr3Cp8gksoIHUuP61pELN8fjTAfXVlfhjBsWonpV4M0RNUQpoiFFYjuc9aWUix+RBFW173I0/55s8OZw3y3Ow==')})
  }
